Men's Health Recommendations: PSA testing annually from age 40. Elevated PSA level doesn't necessarily indicate prostate cancer. Other conditions, such as benign prostatic hyperplasia (BPH) and prostate infections, can also lead to increased PSA levels
Women's Health Recommendations:

Women's Health Recommendations: 
Overview Notes: Liver marker raised. Stop alcohol intake for at least 2-4 weeks and repeat. If still raised do a liver ultrasound.

Sechaba thank you for coming for the medical, well done with all your efforts made so far, I know you will keep improving, hope these tips help you optimise your health.

Overview Notes: Liver marker raised. Stop alcohol intake for at least 2-4 weeks and repeat. If still raised do a liver ultrasound.

Sechaba thank you for coming for the medical, well done with all your efforts made so far, I know you will keep improving, hope these tips help you optimise your health.

Men's Health Recommendations: PSA testing annually from age 40. Elevated PSA level doesn't necessarily indicate prostate cancer. Other conditions, such as benign prostatic hyperplasia (BPH) and prostate infections, can also lead to increased PSA levels
Women's Health Recommendations: 
Overview Notes: Liver marker raised. Stop alcohol intake for at least 2-4 weeks and repeat. If still raised do a liver ultrasound.

Sechaba thank you for coming for the medical, well done with all your efforts made so far, I know you will keep improving, hope these tips help you optimise your health.

Women's Health Recommendations: 
Overview Notes: Liver marker raised. Stop alcohol intake for at least 2-4 weeks and repeat. If still raised do a liver ultrasound.

Sechaba thank you for coming for the medical, well done with all your efforts made so far, I know you will keep improving, hope these tips help you optimise your health.

Men's Health Recommendations: PSA testing annually from age 40. Elevated PSA level doesn't necessarily indicate prostate cancer. Other conditions, such as benign prostatic hyperplasia (BPH) and prostate infections, can also lead to increased PSA levels
Women's Health Recommendations: 
Overview Notes: Liver marker raised. Stop alcohol intake for at least 2-4 weeks and repeat. If still raised do a liver ultrasound.

Sechaba thank you for coming for the medical, well done with all your efforts made so far, I know you will keep improving, hope these tips help you optimise your health.

Comment Key: SpecialInvestigationRecommendation
Comment Value: Normal sinus rhythm, mild electrical alternans, possible U waves on resting ECG 0.5 - 1mm ST depression in inferior leads in recovery phase, no inducible ischaemia. Discuss this with family doctor and check potassium levels

Women's Health Recommendations:
